 Russian President Vladimir Putin told Prime Minister Narendra Modi that the Shanghai Cooperation Organization (SCO) has decided to include India as a full member
 chah deshon vaale is sanghathan ke sammelan se mahaj do din pehle yah baat kahi gai
 During the 90-minute conversation with PM Modi, the host of the SCO conference, Putin said, "we are starting the process to include India as a full member in the SCO
" tippaniyan He said, this is a very important event
 is khabar ke liye putin ko dhanyavad dete hue piem modi ne kaha, bricks ke aapke netritv main, bharat essio kaa sadsy bana he
 i am very grateful
 vartmaan main bharat ke paas sanghathan main paryvekshak kaa darja he
 This six-member organization includes Russia, China, Kazakhstan, Uzbekistan, Kyrgyzstan and Tajikistan
 sanghathan ke anya paryvekshak desh pakistan ko bhi isaki sadsyta milane kii sambhaavna he

 ) Even after the rat was found in the mid-day meal in Delhi's government school, the Kejriwal government may have swung into action and was hastily sending samples from kitchens and schools for investigation, but the reality of the government's food safety department is something else
 is
 sutron kii maane to dilli ke food sefti and security vibhaag main 32 effesao kii jagah he lekin sarkaar ke paas sirf 8 adhikari hai
 The situation is so bad that one of those 8 officers is suspended and the suspension of the other is over, but they are not being given work at the moment
 aise main 33 divijan vaale dilli main khaadya suraksha or usase judy shikayaton kaa nipataara karne kii jimmedaari mahaj 6 khaadya suraksha adhikariyon par hai
 The story does not end here as one of these 6 officers is posted in VIP duty
 yah adhikari viipi ke khaane kii checking ke liedilli polisake saath kaam karata he
 Now only 4 officers are left, out of which, if one goes on leave, then only 3 officers remain in Delhi for complaints like food safety
 dilli sarkaar ke sutron ke mutabik dilli ke 33 divijan ke liye prati divijan 3 adhikariyon kii jarurat he lekin maujuuda haal main mahaj 32 adhikariyon kii hi jagah he
 It has a vacancy of about 24 officers
 jaahir he aise main rajdhani main milawat or khaadya suraksha shikayaton ke niptaare main naa sirf zyada samay lagata he balki kai shikayaton kii sunwaayee or karrwai bhi deree se hoti he
 Deputy Commissioner of the Department Pawan Kamra said that his department is trying to get more and more work with the number of existing officers
 ve adhikariyon kii kami ko sweekaarte hai or kehete hai ki sarkaar ne philhal kai padon par bhartiyon nikaali hai
 However, in the current situation, for the Delhi government, which is facing shortage of officials, the food security of the capital and the disposal of complaints related to it is proving to be a big challenge
 samaj main nahin aata ki logon ne jindagi ko or jindagi ke makasad ko itnaa jatil, itnaa kathin or itnaa rahasyamay kyon bana diya he
 
 
 While it is much more settled, simple and very clearly visible, just like a solid object
 shaayad ham log jindagi ke bare main itane philosafical andaaj main isliye baat karte hai, taaki hamen yah vishwaas ho jaae ki ham jise ji rahe hai, jise apane kandhon par uthaakar chal rahe hai, vah koi choti-moti, saral or halki-phulki cheez nahin he
 Don't you think that by converting such a simple notion into such a forgotten concept, somewhere we are unnecessarily trying to show more of its importance? mere liye to jindagi kii bahut hi saral or vyaavhaarik paribhaasha he
 i do not have enough love to know what a soul is, who i am, where i have come from, why i have come and where i have to go
 mere liye to jindagi utani hi saral, sahaj or spasht he, jitani ki pahadiyon ke bich bahati hui nadi pahadiyon ke liye, aam ke pedo main lagi manjariyaan aam ke ped ke liye, gulab ke paudhon par uge hue tikhe kaante gulab ke liye or lagaataar girti or uthati hui palken ankhon ke liye
 Our idea of self-specificness seems to have complicated our lives
 anyathaa to yah bhi is prakruti kaa usee tarah ek hissaa he, jaise ki chand or sitare hai, pahaad or nadiyaan hai, cheentee or hathi hai or is dharti kii ve sari chijen hai, jo prakruti ne banaai hai
 If we consider ourselves to be part of nature, then it seems very easy to solve the mathematics of life
 mushkil yah he ki ham khud ko prakruti kaa hissaa na samajhakar yah samaj baithe hai ki prakruti hamaara hissaa he
 Or to say that nature is for us
 yadi ek baar ham apane jivan ko vishisht na maanakar prakruti kaa hissaa maan lete hai, to phir hamaare sochane-samajhane kaa najariya hi bilkul badal jaataa he
 Undoubtedly nature has given us the power to think and understand
 lekin hamen is baat ko bhi sochna-samajhnaa hoga ki ham apni is shakti kaa istemaal kar kis tarah se kar rahe hai
 It can be used in this way, it can also be used in any way
 hamaara yah sochna-samajhnaa antat hamen kis nishkarsh tak pahunchayegaa, yah is baat par nirbhar karata he ki ham sochane-samajhane kaa yah kaam kis nazariye se kar rahe hai
 What is our perspective hamaari sochane-samajhane kii kshamta ek gaadi kii tarah he
 Certainly the car is no less important to go somewhere, but where it will go will not decide the steering of the vehicle, but the hands of the driver who operates the steering
 mujhe lagata he ki jaise hi hamaari chetana main yah satya bahut gahare dhans jaataa he ki 'main bhi prakruti kaa ek saamaanya ang hum', vaise hi swayan ko vishisht samajhane kii chetana gaayab ho jaati he, igo nasht ho jaataa he or ankhon ke saamne bane hue ve saare jaale saaf ho jate hai, jo kisi bhi vastu ko spasht rup se dekhne main baadha paidaa kar rahe the
 The comments vaise yadi ham thodaa bhi dhyaan den, to jivan ke is gahare satya ko pakad paane main koi galati nahin hogi ki hamaari adhikansh samasyaon or sankaton kii jad main yah 'igo' naamak khaad hi apana kamaal kar rahaa hota he
 And this 'iago' is nothing else, except to understand oneself as unique
 yahaan gaur karne kii baat yah bhi he ki jab ham itani shaktishaalee or itane viraat prakruti main swayan ko vishisht samaj sakate hai, to phir manushyon kaa vah samaaj to iske saamne chutki bhar bhi nahin he, jisamen rahete hue ham swayan ko vishisht samajhate hai

 is aalekh main di gai kisi bhi soochna kii sateekta, sampoornataa, vyaavhaarikta athwa sachai ke prati enditivi uttaradaayi nahin he

 For me, life is a very simple and practical definition
 meri itani kuwvat nahin he ki main jaan sakuun ki aatma kya he, main koun hum, kahaan se aayaa hum, kyon aayaa hum or kahaan janaa he
 For me, life is as simple, easy and clear as the river flowing between the hills, for the mango trees in the mango trees, for the sharp thorns rose on the rose plants and continuously
 Falling and rising eyelids for eyes
 lagata he ki swayan ko vishisht samajhane ke hamaare vichaar ne hamaare jivan ko jatil banaaya he
 Otherwise, it is also a part of this nature, just like there are moons and stars, mountains and rivers, ants and elephants and all the things on this earth that nature has created
 yadi ek baar ham apane ko prakruti kaa hi hissaa samaj lete hai, to phir jivan ke ganit ko suljhaana bahut aasaan lagane lagata he
 The difficulty is that we do not consider ourselves to be part of nature and understand that nature is part of us
 yaa ise yun kah lijie ki prakruti hamaare liye he
 If once we consider our life as not part of nature, then our attitude of thinking changes completely
 nihsandeh prakruti ne hi hamen sochane-samajhane kii shakti di he
 But we also have to think and understand how we are using this power
 iskaa istemaal is tarah bhi ho saktaa he, us tarah bhi ho saktaa he or kisi bhi tarah ho saktaa he
 How far our thinking and understanding will ultimately lead us to depends on how we are doing this thinking and understanding
 hamaara drushtikon kya he
 Our ability to think is like a car
 nishchit taur par kahin jane ke liye gaadi kam mahatvapurn nahin he, lekin vah jaaegi kahaan, is baat kaa faisla gaadi kaa steering nahin karegaa, balki driver ke ve haath karenge, jo steering ko sanchalit karte hai
 i think that as soon as the truth is deeply ingrained in our consciousness that 'I am also a normal part of nature', in the same way, the consciousness of understanding itself disappears, the ego is destroyed and before the eyes All the webs that are made are cleared, which were hindering the seeing of any object clearly
 tippaniyan By the way, if we pay even a little attention, there will be no mistake in catching this deep truth of life that at the root of most of our problems and crises, this manure called 'ego' is doing its job
 or yah 'igo' kuch or nahin he, sivaay khud ko vishisht samajhane ke
 It is also a matter to note here that when we can understand ourselves as so powerful and so special in such a vast nature, then the society of human beings is not even a pinch in front of it, in which while living we consider ourselves special

 Security officials revealed this on Wednesday
 airbas e330-300 vimaan 10 march ko sidney se uda or kualalampur ke raste par tha
 Meanwhile, air traffic control was alerted when the aircraft started flying in the wrong direction
 jaanch ke baad australian transport suraksha beuro (atisbi) ne bataaya, 'air trephic ne vimaan ke kru ko soochna de di lekin samasya ko dur karne kii koshish kaa nateeja neyvigation system, vimaan ke flite gidence or flite control system main or zyada giravat ke rup main saamne aayaa
 The pilot then decided to return to Sydney but was forced to fly to Melbourne due to bad weather where the aircraft landed safely
 payalat 18 maheene se A330 vimaan uda rahaa tha
 The ATSB found that while setting the flight management and guidance system of the aircraft, the wrong longitudinal position of the aircraft was accidentally recorded
 'isse neyvigation system par vipareet asar hua
 Although there were many opportunities to identify and rectify the mistake, it was not noticed until the aircraft started flying in the wrong direction
 ' The ATSB also found that the aircraft did not have an upgrade version of the flight management system, which prevents incorrect data entry
 atisbi ne kaha, vimaan ke kru ne samasya ko dur karne kii koshish bhi kii
 But due to the limited guidelines from the current checklist, the mistake was more than corrected
 saath hi atisbi ne bataaya ki sasti yatra ke liye jaani jane vaali malaysian airline ne is ghatana ko apane sabhi payalton ke saath saajha kiya or apane flite kru ke liye ek nayaa training minial bhi vikisat kiya

 CMSEO ne kaha tha ki somvaar ko antariksh prayogshaala (spes lab) prithvi ke vayumandal main dobaaraa pravesh karegaa
